<Author>pvm
<Content>beautiful beach  I was at this hotel from Dec 4th to the 12th. The weather was fantastic except for the last day which rained. Okay lets get into the resort itself. It currently changed management and went from LTI Punta Cana to VIK Arena Blanca, what i was told was that when this happened more than half the staff was let go. They are in the process of renovating the rooms. My check in was fast and we were given 2 rooms close by. To be honest i was not really disappointed with the resort, not like i have read in some of the reviews but again everyone has their own expectations and tastes.Ok the rooms, we were in building 2 which has not yet been renovated as they are doing one building at a time. My room was clean, the bed was not too bad and i did not have such a bad view. I will agree that they hotel does not provide any washcloths so bring your own as well as bring your own soap as they have liquid soap in the bathroom. I know some people have complained about the noise but to be honest the construction noise is only during the day and it truly is not that bad that it bothers you. I really have no complaints about the quality of the pillows or bed as i slept without any problems every night. Food was not bad at all. I always found something to eat and the pizza at the beach bar is fantastic. It was always fresh and yummy. I also loved the bbq chicken and was always saved a piece at lunch by the cook. The service is not bad at all and i tipped daily and to be honest was remembered and service was always provided very promptly as well as with a smile. Tipping a dollar here and there is not required by any means but always appreciated by the staff.Ok now to the beach and pool. The beach is absolutely beautiful, white sands and the water is wonderful and warm. I never had any problems getting a chair to lounge on at any time of the day. I know that the beach the little huts get taken fast in the morning but there is always some shade so there is no problems at all. As for the pool you can always get shade and sun at any time of the day. The activity team is always doing something so there is always some fun activities happening. If you do want to go shopping there are some shops on the beach about 4 mins from the hotel and we called it Tent city, be prepared to bargain and you can get some good deals. Dont be put off by some of the negative reviews. If you dont expect the Ritz you will enjoy yourself. The beach is beautiful and the grounds are kept very clean and nice. People are friendly and they do speak English at the front desk as well as the bars and restaurants, i had no problems what so ever. The food was always good and i never went without eating or got sick from the food or drinks. Overall my experience with this resort was not bad at all. I enjoyed it and would go back in the future maybe once most of the renovations are done.

<Author>Vicki_Gordon
<Content>Consider it 'Just OK for me' Travel Dates: December 3-11/08.This was our annual girls week away to Punta Cana. We chose the VIK because I knew of the location (right next door to the PCP which I stayed in 3 months ago). The price for this trip was $397.00 plus taxes ($308.00). We booked it to include oceanview in advance so we knew exactly what we should be expecting when we arrived.Arrival: We arrived on time without any winter delays this year. Our arrival at the resort was very what I would call out of the ordinary. I must preface this by saying that I have been to the Dominican 10 times over the last 3 years and have stayed in many different resorts in both Puerta Plata and Punta Cana. On our arrival at the VIK, we were not greeted by anyone, we had the bus driver point for us to go to the desk, and were not given any type of drink after our long journey. I though oh, well, this nicety was just forgotten or missed. What we really did not know, was that this is really the norm at this resort. None of the employees seemed happy or even happy to have us at the resort. It was a strange feeling. Unfortunatey, I know that this is my review, but the sentiment was felt by everyone else that we spoke to at the resort as well. I am used to seeing the employees dancing and singing and smiling all or most of the time. I did not see this AT ALL at this resort. It was kind of a strange feeling. Anyway, back to our arrival...........We received our room information, and it was exactly as I had asked for. We were in building 5 on the second floor facing the ocean. It was a beautiful view and I was very impressed. Our Room: It was very very clean and well presented but dated. The hotel is currently in the process of renovating the rooms, one block at a time. I was not at all disappointed in the room. As others have indicated, it was a little stange to have half of the bathroom door with a window for all to see. The actual toilet area was kind of tucked around the corner of the bathroom, so not quite in the total view of everyone. You had one sink in the bathroom with your standard shower area. You have 2 bath towels and 2 hand towels.....so if you use facecloths, bring your own. Do not expect any other amenities...........bring all of your own soaps, shampoos, creams, etc...........you will not get anything here. Out of the 7 days we were there, we only had what I would call hot water 2 of those days. The other 5 was luke warm at the very best. The storage spaces are adequate. One side of the entrance to the bathroom is a closest which holds the safe and a place to put your clothes, the other side is another closet which has a place to put your suitcases and hanger space for more clothing. The dresser in the room has 4 drawers (good size) and a bar fridge. In the fridge, you receive 2 large bottles of water, 2 coke, 2 sprite which are replenished daily. The beds are ok, but very low to the ground. It felt funny having them at knee level. I had to ask for an additional blanket because I get cold in the night with the air conditioning. The pillows are the worst I have ever slept on anywhere in my life. I do not know how to stress that any stronger. They are made out of chip foam and stuffed into what looks like a pillow. I had to have four of them around my head to have half a decent nights sleep. If you have any spare room in your luggage, bring your own. The daily cleaning of the room was ok, with the exception of one day, they did not come until 6:30 at night. I just asked for clean towels and sent them along their way. You do not get any nice touches to your room as I have received at any of the other resorts that we have ever stayed in. I also found that a little strange as we always left money every day for the housekeeping staff. We did not have TV for 2 days as they lost their satelite. We did not have a TV converter for 5 days as they had run out.Food: Good and bad.........The breakfast buffets were what you would expect from any resort. The lunch at the pool was very good. They had a great BBQ for lunch every day with Chicken, hambergs and hotdogs etc. They also had a pizza oven, and it was very good. The dinner buffets were very poor. No carving stations, they had a small pasta bar, a chinese section. By the time you had your food back at the table it was always cold. You had to get your water for yourself most of the time since staff were never really around. The tables were often dirty and you had to wait for them to be cleared often to sit down. If you finished your meal and went to get desert, your dirty diner dishes often stayed on your table for the rest of your stay. In comparison to every other resort I stayed at, the staff were always there to take your dishes away as soon as your pushed it aside or if your water glass was half empty, it was always filled. NOT HERE. This was very very disappointing to me. No exceptional service at all. To me, this makes or breaks a resort. Never once did I see a happy face welcoming us to diner.Beach and Pool: All I can say is excellent. That is why we chose this resort. Lots of beach chairs, and shaded areas. Never once did we have to play the chair game.Overall: I would not return to this resort. It was not a bad experience, but not a great one either. As far as recommending it. Just be aware. If you do not care about service, go for it. The weather was good, and the fun we had at the Tower Casino made up for the resort.

<Author>PickyTraveller77
<Content>Will go back ANY day! When we arrived, the LTI was undergoing a management change. It is now called VIK Arena Blanca. Some things might get better or worsen, it is difficult to say but overall, we had a wonderful experience. I was travelling with 3 other girl friends with extensive travel experience and we all have been to several resorts, all ratings, in the past. We tend to be picky but wanted a cheaper vacation this time. We would GO BACK!In summary: NEW, CLEAN, GREAT SIZE, GREAT PEOPLE, LOTS OF ACTIVITY OPTIONS.This is a small-ish resort. When we arrived, there was no band playing or special drinks or anything like this but we were greeted by very friendly people at the reception who called the waiter to offer us a cerveza! It was very kind. We then headed over to our rooms.There is not too much walking to get to the room or to the restaurants/beach. Everything is nearby and all services are available. A 3-minute walk will bring you to the gym, medical clinic, spa or the casino (a small one).ROOM: It was VERY CLEAN, the bathrooms are nice, it's all marble, new tubs, toilets, etc. The only weird thing is that the door has a window in it but we dealt with it by hanging our towel in it! BEDS: comfortable but here is a tip: BRING YOUR OWN PILLOW. I noticed some rooms seem to have normal pillows but for us, it was those little half pillows and the foam in it was in thousands of little pieces so it was not very comfortable. We did not have an oceanview room or anything like this, but all rooms on the resort have a nice view anyway! The balconies are very nice and they have new furniture on them too (nothing fancy but nice). There is A/C, fan.WEATHER: It was very hot during the day and at night, cool enough to wear a little sweater. The nice thing is that we only had our fan on and no need to turn on the A/C! Very comfortable weather. In the DR in regular season, it rains for a few minutes and it is sunny again. It happened twice only and it was nighttime.RESTAURANTS: Only TWO a-la-cartes; NO reservations necessary. Service was extremely slow and food was not that good. I saw pictures from the old LTI and it may have been better back then. The Estrella del Mar serves different fish/meats and the Trattoria (Italian) is pasta or meats. Vegetarian options as well. Filet Meunier at Estrella was swimming in butter! Don't recommend it but other dishes looked good. Oven macaroni at Italian was like Kraft Dinner. I would recommend the the lasagna. We waited in line since they don't do reservations: go early or be prepared to wait.They alternate the restaurants (one night it is Italian that's open, the following night it's the fish one).BUFFET: It wasn't the worst we had, but definitely not the best as in nothing fancy. If you are a PICKY EATER, you will find a lot of things you like. No theme nights, just a bit of everything every night. Pasta, stir fries (they make them for you), paella, lots of meats, fish, potatoes, rice dishes. Lots of fruit, vegetables. Desserts are ok. Breakfast: EVERYTHING, EVERY DAY.LUNCH/SNACK BAR: It's the food place for lunch starting at 11 until 6:30pm. The pizza is DELICIOUS. They make hamburgers and hot dogs and there is also a mini buffet inside (you can also do the buffet at lunch). It is just around the pool. You can take your plate pretty much anywhere. There was a paella chef once during our stay and that was great! DRINKS: A few bars, very clean. You know the ice cubes are made with filtered water too!WATER: You can fill up your water bottles by any bars. They have fountains with filtered water.The coffee machine in the lobby makes the BEST CAPPUCCINOS and CAFE con leche. We had several of those!! Good tea selection in little baskets. If you like peppermint, take a few bags when you see them: they go fast! If you like larger quantities of tea/water/drinks, BRING YOUR OWN BIG MUG!! STAFF: Friendly if you make friends with them. Otherwise, not as friendly (surprisingly). However, they will always help if you ask.ANIMATION: Great team! Very nice, lots of fun, lots of activities. Music wasn't great though and people didn't participate as much as on other resorts.GUESTS/NIGHTLIFE: If you want to party, don't go there. It's dead at night. Crowd is mostly Germans, Canadians, a few south americans, French. Age group older than ours (40+) however there were a few of us under 35. You need to go outside of the resort if you want a nightclub. There's 1 bar at night and a disco that are usually....not very crowded.BEACH: I would compare it to the Bahamas beach (Paradise island) if you've been. Little waves, you can walk for miles and miles on the beach and the water does not get deep quickly, bottom is clear, seaweed free except for 1 day that they all seemed to have come at once but it's a BEAUTIFUL beach, for ANY resort you go to that's on Bavaro Beach. Overall for the price that we paid, we had a WONDERFUL vacation and it was just what we were looking for!

<Content>LTI was just OK..more like a 3 star  Stayed at the LTI (Also known as the VIK arena blanca) Nov. 17- 24th. There is a large selection of alcohol and drink menus, and the buffet does have a variety of foods.However! I have never had such horrible service before. You are best to go to Cancun or Varadero for a party scene..To sum up my review, I will say that Punta Cana is a beautiful destination with so many other amazing resorts you can stay at- for example the Paradisus or the Bahia chain are incredible., stay away from this resort and spend the extra $200 for an incredible 4 or 5 star on the beach.

<Author>colbie
<Content>SO much fun! I visited this resort as a graduation present in December of last year, and was pleasantly surprised by it! Let me break it down for you:The Grounds: Beautiful gardens. Connecting cobblestone pathways throughout the entire resort. Spa on site (a little expensive, but still good). Geckos running through occassionally. The Room: Basic, but satisfactory. We had a gardenview room, with an excellent view of the sunset at night. The one and only complaint is that the air conditioner leaked.The Beach: Bavaro Beach is the most BEAUTIFUL beach I have ever seen! This resort is right on the beach, at a prime section of it. No matter what time you get there, there is always a lounge chair or spot available to sit or lie down, often under an umbrella. At some sections of the beach, there are waves, and at others the water is completely calm. About a five minute walk to the left of the resort along the beach, there is a really cool flea market, where you can shop and barter away to your hearts content (I picked up a huge $8 bottle of rum, $4 sunglasses, and other trinkets). The Food/Drinks:The food at LTI is quite good. For breakfast there is a huge buffet with fresh fruit, cereal, eggs, yummy croissants etc. For lunch, there is always a BBQ going with hamburgers, hot dog, chicken, and the special fish of the day. And for dinner, you have the choice of two buffets, or two delicious a-la-carte restaurants (italian and seafood). There are also at least 3 bars that I can recall visiting at the resort. One right on the beach, and one at each buffet site (but I'm sure there was more). Ask for a Bahama Mama with white rum.. they are the best! Activities:To be honest, I mainly lay around on the beach, but the resort, and the nearby vendors offered many acivity options including:-parasailing-spa-internet access-boat rides-snorkeling -scuba diving-yoga-water aerobics-dance lessons-market shopping-jungle excursions-photo shoots (free! it's your choice if you want to purchase any pictures from it.)-and more

<Author>avoorhees
<Content>Great Stay at LTI Just back a week ago from a week stay at the LTI Beach Resort  Spa in Punta Cana. We had a great stay and would definitely recommend this hotel. We found all of the staff very helpful (especially Manuel at reception!). I'll just add a few things that we found that I didn't see covered in other reviews... We ended up not arranging for transportation before we left and had no problem at all. There are tons of taxis avail. at the airport in clearly marked vehicles. We were quoted prices $40 - $38. We found one taxi group that would take us for $35. We ended up taking a taxi back to the airport as well and it was $38. The trip takes about a half hour. We never changed money, everyone took U.S dollars or euros. As suggested by other reviews, we requested Building 4 or 5 when we arrived. As of August 8, 2008 Building 5 is considered 'superior' and would be $25 additional per person per night and Buidling 4 is currently under construction. They ended up showing us a couple of rooms to let us choose and we choose one in Building 3. Of the rooms we were shown, we choose one on the 3rd floor (the top) because it had a vaulted ceilng so felt a lot bigger and the air seemed to move a bit better. Buidling 3 was very centrally located, but one of the great aspects of this hotel is that nothing is very far. There is the main buffet restaurant and 2 a la carte restaurants. We were there in the off season so the a la carte restaurants did not require a reservation but still did have a dress code (long pants for men, no sandals, etc.). Since we enjoyed the beach so much, we just ended up taking one excursion. We did the Carribean Festival which included great snorkeling and then swimming with nurse sharks and interacting with sting rays. It was $78 per person for a half day and definitely worth it. You can also get snorkeling gear for an hour a day at the beach activities buidling but there is a roped off swimming area (lots of boats going by) so not much to see. You can also sign up for a catamaran ride once per stay. The shops are a pretty short walk down the beach (one hotel over) and the haggeling over prices is pretty fun! They also have a couple of tables set up a couple of nights right at the hotel with jewelry and cigars. We did actually find that the little end shop set up permanently by the pool (connected to the t-shirt shop) had really great prices for jewelry.We enjoyed our stay and think that the beach was one of the best we've visited. The room was clean and had everything we needed (even if the beds were really hard!). The minibar was stocked every day (w 2 lg. bottles of water, 2 cokes, 2 sprites). We came back very relaxed and with very good memories of the DR.

<Author>doctorpatrick
<Content>Paradise! I've read the critical reviews and couldn't disagree more. First, if you check the prices on other Punta Cana all inclusives you'll see that this resort is a genuine bargain. True, the rooms are somewhat dated but charming (and clean) nevertheless. Bug free too. The staff is very helpful and friendly ( grateful for the smallest tip), the food is varied  delicious, the shows amusing and, hey, the bars (free drinks) are open around the clock. The pools are some of the best I've ever seen. The beach has to be experienced to be believed. Probably one of the best in the Caribbean! One word of caution. If you hate topless European women stay away! I can understand the complaints about plumbing and electrical problems but this is the Dominican Republic (as in third world country, duh) . If you can't handle it go to the Jersey Shore next time! Please note that as of November '08 LTI will be changing its name to VIK Hotel Arena Blanca. Have fun and don't complain about a good thing!

<Author>Tardykat
<Content>Good value. Friendly staff. My girlfriends and I took a week-long trip here. I loved the way we were greeted, welcome home they said. We booked the package which included ground transfer from Club Caribe. Club Caribe offers excursions. We met our CC advisor the next morning to discuss options and confirm our booking. Make sure you print 2 copies of the ground transfer voucher as they took one copy when we arrived and then they needed it again for our return.The rooms were basic garden view with 2 twin beds. When my friend called to confirm her booking she requested for their best room and was upgraded to an ocean view room just like that! The property is small, you can get from your room to anywhere (buffet, lobby, pool, beach) in about 5 minutes. The rooms are spread out in 5 buildings (1 to 5) with #5 closest to the beach and 1 closest to the front of the property. We were in #2 (ground floor room) and my friend with the ocean view was #4 (3rd floor room). #2 and #3 building was in the middle of the property, which I think is ideal. There is a section on the side reserved only for Cayena Beach Club members (time share users) it includes a pool and a restaurant. Their rooms were better, we took a tour after listening to a long talk about becoming members. If you don't want to waste 2 hours of your time, don't get grabbed to go to one of these talks.The rooms are bare but sufficient for laying your head at night. Beware of mosquitoes at night if you leave your balcony door open. There was a fan/AC/hair dryer in our room and 2 bottles of water, Sprite and Coke in the fridge, restocked daily. Bring soap/shampoo/conditioner as the gel used in the bathrooms are those 3 in 1 types that leave your hair stiff.There are 2 small restaurants which require reservations the morning of. The food there was ok. We preferred the international buffet. The fresh papaya milk shakes during breakfast was awesome! There is also an all-day BBQ by the pool with the most tender chicken I've ever had. The bartenders are not cheap with the alcohol for the drinks. We took advantage of the free use of kayaks. There are also sailing catamarans but we didn't get the chance.The Animacion staff are amazing. They keep the atmosphere festive. Did encounter some surly staff at the buffet seating area but overall, everyone was very friendly. The nightly shows are a bit corny but are fun. Majority of the guests were European so it wasn't surprising to see topless women.I think the palm trees look the best on LTI's beachfront as there are several that are bent nearly to the ground and you can climb up and photograph with them. The water is the Atlantic so a bit rough for us amateurs. It is also not crystal clear due to the rough surf. We spent most of our time in the pool.I would stay here again.

We would find 鈥渙ur鈥?hut each morning and place our towels on the chair on the way to breakfast. The stores are VERY expensive, however, our primary reason for going was the Hard Rock Caf茅. The prices are comparable to other Hard Rocks around the world. The sales people are aggressive and after a while will take a no. Be sure to barter, and you will be surprised how low they will go. Although the music normally was, I鈥檓 just not into dancing for 7 nights in a row. After leaving the disco, we would head to the beach to enjoy our final drinks and call it a night. It was the smoothest I鈥檝e ever experienced.This trip was by far our best, and we look forward to another return in the fall of this year. If you have any questions, please let me know, I鈥檓 more than happy to assist!

<Author>disneynutmdf
<Content>Overall, better than average Our family of five, my husband and I in our 40's and three kids age 13, 12, and 5, stayed here April 21-28. Overall I would have to say our stay was better than average, but you have to take the good with the bad, plan ahead, and make it your own vacation. It helped immensely that I spoke Spanish. We visited from the US and we were definitely the minority. A lot of German and French/Canadian at the resort. My husband is very high spirited, so it helped in making our vacation fun. He enjoyed playing beach volleyball with our daughters and others. My son enjoyed the kids club, and the staff from the kids club really made an effort to get the kids involved. My son absolutely loved Pablo and to this day is still saying that he misses him.check in and the rooms.....Check in went smooth for us, however, I had emailed the resort several times prior to our arrival with requests for our family due to medical conditions my 5 year old faces. Our request were partially met. They did not have connecting rooms at this resort so they put us in a family suite (although we had the option of two rooms right next to each other but the thought of our kids in one room and us in the other just didn't float with us, even if it was just right next to us), for more reasons than one...safety, medical issues with our son, two beautiful girls in a foreign country, the age of our children.....etc...etc..... A family suite only had one bathroom which was a down side to it all, not to mention that the master room was also the living room so we had no privacy. But, because we didn't want to leave the kids in a room of their own, and we didn't want to split the family up on a family vacation, we decided to take the family suite. On the plus side, we had a beautiful ocean view and got the free upgrade. Rafael at the front desk was extremely professional and courteous. Given one can only work with what you are given and he can only give out the rooms given at the resort....he can't make something magically appear that isn't there...the situation was well handled and he gave us the best two case scenarios and let us decide what we wanted for our family. I think it definitely helps that we emailed ahead of time...several times...and made our request well known. It's true what some other reviews say about the bathrooms having windows panes as the upper half of the door. We asked for thumbtacks at the front desk and hung a towel up with them to resolve that problem. We did encounter a problem getting hot water....it was warm at it's best, but pressure was good. No plugs for the tub, so bathing my son, I had to run the shower, but the nozzle for the shower was a removable one, and used it. Rented the lock for the safe to secure our more important items such as jewlery, ipods, wallets and passports. They did fumigate...I refused due to my son's medical condition just didn't want to take any chances. My son slept on the sofa bed. One morning after he was given a comforter to cover himselft with by housekeeping, he woke up scratching a lot with tiny bumps on him. I have to be honest and say that I don't know if it was due to bedbugs from the comforter (he didn't have them the previous two nights on the sofabed so they didn't come from there) or if they were a reaction he could've had to the sunscreen I was using on hime as he is sensitive to a lot of things. I will never find out. I do know that I never used the comforter again, and they seemed to go away although he scratched for two days and being I came prepared for him, I had benadryl as well as Benadryl gel I could apply to his skin. I continued to use the sunscreen because I really didn't think it had come from that since he's used it all his life. He played a lot in the sand as well....so who knows.Food....adequate but nothing to brag home about. Breakfast was good. My son liked the omelettes. Not the kind we are used to here in the states, but still good. pancakes available, bacon, sausage, potatotes, crepes, a few cereals, yogurts, fruit, fruitshakes (bannana, pineapple, papaya, and melon). A lot of breakfast choices. My husband loved the chicken at lunch by the beach grill. The buffet for lunch was average at best, but always something could still be found. Two out of five of us had stomach problems and three of us did not. Funny thing was that those of us that usually have weak stomachs at home were the ones that were fine on the trip. The breads morning noon and night along with breadsticks and flatbreads were delicious and quite surprisingly good. My husband really enjoyed the chinese stations. I had a little bit one night and thought it was good too.The Italian place only had pizza, no other specialty dishes, but the pizza was good and so was the service. The seafood place only had one fish plate that was included...anything else was available for a price of at least $28 american or so and I didn't enjoy the lobster in the white sauce and then back into it's shell. I forget what it was called. It was prepared with the lungs and all and had a very weird taste and the next morning was the only day I actually had stomach problems.The pool and beach. The pool was clean the entire time we were there and my son loved it. The water was nice. The jacuzzi temperature was the same temperature as the pool water. The beach was spectacular. Cleaned every day from seaweed and the water gorgeous aquamarine and warm (low 80's). The sand pinkish white and soft and we just loved it. Played many beach games. Did a snorkeling excursion through the hut to the left of the hotel where you can book on the beach which was average but then got our wristbands stamped and had unlimitted use of snorkeling gear, kayaks, boogieboards, etc for the week. My kids had a blast with the boogie boards. Even though the waves are no where big enough for boogie boarding, they still had a fun time. Plenty of lounge chairs on the beach. If you want one under a beach hut, you better be up by 6:30pm!!! One of the excursions you can book from the hut on property or the hut over by the water sports talks about visiting a giant inflatable slide. This slide is actually a public slide set up on the beach at the Fiesta Resort. As you face the ocean, you take a right and walk the beach to get to the Fiesta Resort. It's quite a walk (about 20 or 25 minutes), but we took it and it was well worth it to get to the water slide. The kids loved the slide...they spray water down the slide and you prior to going down the slide so it then becomes a water slide. You pay X amount and then get to go down the slide an specific amount of times depending on the amount you pay. I believe we payed $10 for 14 slides. They give you 14 rubberbands you can put around your wrist and they take one away every time you slide down once. You can also pay $5 for 6 slides. The kids had a blast and my husband and I even went down a few times and enjoyed it. It was one of the highlights for my 5 and 12 year old. You can take a taxi to the resort, but then I guess to get onto the beach you would have to explain once you got to the Fiesta resort how you wish to use the water slide located on their beach and I would think it shouldn't be a problem. Afterall, it's not like the resort would serve you their food or drinks if you don't have a wristband from their resort.Other excursions.....My husband and daughters did the 4X4 excursion that can be booked at the hut over by where the towels are given out. It was the best price he could find and he looked around a bit. They told him it was a three hour excursion. He and the girls said they really had a good time. What they fail to tell you is that it takes over 2 hrs to get to the place because they stop for other folks at other hotels along the way. On the way back they said it was quicker but still a bit of a way. They left the hotel at 1:30pm and I was actually at the front desk asking if they could please find out where they were and all because I was very worried about them since it was 6:30pm and they still weren't back from what was supposed to have been a 3 hour excursion. As a mother and wife one worries and you think the worse. I was glad to see them when they got back and they said it was a fun time, but they were dissapointed that the time to get there and back was so long and that no one told them when booking.We have been to Punta Cana before. We love the beach there. We have stayed at other resorts that are nicer. I must say that this is a good resort if you have younger kids. Two of the other resorts I stayed at I did not see the animation staff get as involved with the kids as I saw here. Granted, they are gone from noon to 2 or 3pm and then again from 5pm to 8:30pm and then they have a little kids show on the stage for 1/2 hour for them, but when they are around, they keep them entertained very well. They don't have a club per say. They just do activities. Their club is an outdoor playground with a covered terrace. Nothing with an indoor playroom with airconditioning or anything of the sort. When I went next door to the Ocean Blue to check out their grounds with my husband....they had much bigger grounds...so big that they have a tram to get you around...but they also had a nice club for the children..an actual playroom with airconditioning...etc. They had a rock climbing wall for the kids at Ocean Blue as well as a trampoline. But.....bigger isn't always better. Although I would go for bigger next time as our kids will be older and it would be nicer, when we walked through the bigger resort at two different places (Fiesta and Ocean Blue, both our daughters commented how they were happy they were staying in a smaller place where they didn't have to walk so much to get to things and how it just felt safer for them. You do get a better feel. It's hard to explain. I did see security guards on the beach at all the resorts, although I have to say, for whatever the reason, LTI seemed to have more than the other resorts.Would I go back to LTI, probably not, but not because of any major problems....just because there are so many other places in Punta Cana that I would like to try as well.

I did tend to use the omelet bar and pasta bar the most as then you can be assured of fresh food. They even let us in one night when we didn't have reservations.The beach was definately the highlight with beautiful white sand (like talcum powder) that extended all the way out into the swimming area. We spent the majority of our time on the beach or playing in the waves.I found the staff very friendly and the only ones I found a bit short were the ones working at the front desk. Everyone else was more than willing to say hola and smile.The market down the beach was a great source of bartering and we went back several times - it was located on the other side of the Ocean Sands resort which was next to LTI. I had my hairbraided at the end closest to LTI and they shared cold beer with me the entire time as it was one of the girl's birthday. We liked the LTI resort as it was small and we could easily split up our group and then meet up later on the beach. We heard several people on our flight home complain that their resorts were too big and they were difficult to get around. Having walked up and down the beach, I would say LTI has one of the nicest beach areas. I would definately recommend LTI to others.

<Author>UpstateNY_8
<Content>Would go back again! Just returned from LTI with my husband and our 2 boys (18, 11). We consider ourselves seasoned Caribbean travelers, as my husband works for a major airline. There were no surprises at LTI. It is one of the smaller resorts, however the grounds are beautifully maintained, the beach is wonderful, and the free form pool is great. We had a family suite(2 twin beds as you walk in the door, separated by a door leading into another bedroom with a king bed) which offered a gorgeous view overlooking the ocean and the pool area. Yes, the rooms are VERY basic, with VERY basic amenities-and yes, we found that the pillows are lumpy so we requested more, and they were quickly brought to our room. Although we thought it was time the rooms could use an overhaul, i.e., paint, plaster repairs, etc...the maids kept them clean. What we were very surprised about was the food. We really thought there was a great selection and it was great! The shows were nice, the animation team was very friendly, and we felt the same way for the majority of the staff who were always hard at work. If you are looking for a Ritz, this isn't the place for you, nor does LTI pretend to be. If you are looking for a great pool, beach area, and laid back resort at a good value, this is the place.....we would go back, as we truly enjoyed our stay. Upstate, NY

<Content>Really a 4.5 star resort My husband and I stayed at the LTI Beach Resort February 15-22, 2008. We were really concerned about the reviews on the resort we read before we left for Dominican, but we assure you won't be disappointed in this resort!Though we purchased our trip as a 4 star resort, it could easily pass for 4.5 star. We stayed in building 1, which is the furthest from the beach, but not far at all in comparison to other places we have been, since the resort itself is quite contained. Our room was beautiful, on the 2nd floor, very clean, with a mini fridge which was filled with pop and water everyday. Air conditioning worked really well (almost too well to keep it on all night long). Food was great, lots of choices and always somewhere to eat. We really liked the food at the seafood restaurant however there isn't much seafood on the menu. The pizza at the Italian Restaurant is terrific thin crust yumminess, however the menu is really limited to only pizzas. The buffet food is fine too, however we always found it really busy if we tried to eat supper there, so preferred the a la carte for that reason. The crossants in the breakfast buffet are to die for and so is the fresh pineapple juice. Near the beach there is a lunchtime BBQ with chicken and burgers. My husband loved the BBQ chicken. Also, late night after the entertainment there is a pannini station by the bar which has excellent sandwitches. We really liked the cappucchinos in the lobby bar area too.We are beach people so spent everyday at the beach. THE BEACH IS BEAUTIFUL! We could always find a couple loungers in the shade though sometimes it did required some hunting. Great swimming and they clean any seaweed off the beah everyday. The walk down the beach is also beautiful, and about 10 minutes down the beach there are a bunch of vendors set up selling the usual fare.The pool looked nice, but we didn't spend any time there to be honest.The evening shows were really high quality. The Michael Jackson show was fabulous.We went to the gym a few times and it was pretty good as far as resort gyms go, but very basic. A couple cardio machines, some free weights, and a few weight machines.We only went to the disco one night, and it was ok, but very small. The grounds are absolutely impeccably kept. We wished we had booked for two weeks instead of one.

<Author>Bootsy16
<Content>Lti was fantastic Me and my boyfriend stayed at the Lti for two weeks starting 24th september 07. We are both in our early 20's and went for a relaxing break. Here is what we thought:The Rooms: We stayed in block 4. When we first got to the room we were very pleased with it. I requested a room overlooking the pool and we got it. The bathrooms are very nice too, apart from the doors have glass in them so you can see into them but the toilet is out of view. They have a hair dryer in them which works quite well. We had a TV but no remote, we phoned the reception desk and they got one for us straight away. Our patio doors didn't lock either and we did tell reception a few times but they never got round to fixing it. So never leave anything valuble in the room. There was a fridge in the room and every day the maids would re stock it for us free of charge, we would get two bottles of coke, two bottles of sprite and two large bottles of water. The good thing about this hotel too is that the ice and all the water they use is made from purified water so its safe to drink it and not get sick. We read a few reviews which told us to tip the maid as they would leave nice things around the room, we left a dollar a day and they made things out of the towels and put flowers in it, they also gave us extra pillows. The beach: The beach was lovely, white sands and blue sea. Get there reasonably early if you want a chairs. They do lots of activities on the beach; football, volleyball etc. I never spent much time on the beach as i don't like to swim in the sea! But a few days we walked down it and there are some huts to the left where you can buy souveniers. The people there are very pushy and try and charge you lots of money, work out how much your money is worth compared to theirs then choose how much you are willing to pay. They tried to charge me 拢10 for a plastic bracelet, in the end i got the bracelet, earrings and two neclaces for 拢5. All the huts sell the same things too. The pool: The pool was nice, there are two, the kiddy pool is closer to the beach then there's a larger one the closer to the lobby. We spent the first week by the larger one, during the day the animation team would be in charge of lots of activities. They will come round and ask you to join in but if you say no they don't pester you. We joined in a few of the games and if you win you have to go on stage at the evening entertainment and you get a bottle of really strong drink, rum or something?? And they make you do a dance! Quite embarrasing. They also play music this side of the pool as this is where the animation teams hut is. They play the same songs every day which can get a bit annoying after a week. Every morning and night you do see a few men cleaning out the pool and it is generally clean. At about 11 each morning two men teach scuba diving, this is free, just walk up to them and they'll tell you when they are free to teach you. The food/bars: The main buffet is brilliant, they have such a huge range of food. You walk in and its all set out in a circle, Be carfeul about what you choose as some doesn't look cooked, we never got ill. Around the outside there are food stations, you can pick out the ingredients and they cook it infront of you, these were very nice. They do breakfast lunch and dinner here. You have to go to the italian, we went there nearly every other night, the pizza's were lovely. You get the food and drinks brought to you. It's only open a couple of nights a week and you can book with somebody sitting at the desk near the main buffet at breakfast. If you don't eat it all you can ask for it to be put into a box and you can take it away. The lunch by the pool is ok if you don't want to get dressed to go into the buffet as they wont let you in with wet shorts and you have to have a top on. They do burgers chips and hotdogs. The chips are nice but the meat just looks fatty and greasy, one day i got a burger that was pink on the inside. I tried not to eat the meat and just had pasta and things. You could also eat one night a week on the beach, it looked very nice but we never did it as it clashed with trips we had booked. The bars are a bit slow, and none of them speak english so try and learn numbers in spanish or just make hand gestures as to how many you want, The things that look like slush puppies in the machines are banana mumma and pina colada, they will ask you if you want rum with it. These were very nice. The bar immediatly by the pool in a little white shack was horrible, there were lots of wasps flying around, the bar man never seemed bothered that they were sitting on his head but you could never order a drink easily as they are flying around your head and flying around the coke machine and in drinks. You can also get rolls and soup in the bar by the pool tables throughout the night, this is good when you come out of the disco and have a craving for something to eat although pizza would be better. Trips: The trips were fun, we went swimming with sharks and sting rays, this was a good one, you go out on a catamaran and swim with the fish, they provide you with snorkle equipment, then you pull up to an enclosure in the sea and swim with the sharks,  on the way back to shore the staff dress up and hand out drinks and everybody dances. We also went to saona island, this was a long day,you get a coach to a beach and stop at hotels along the way, you drive through tiny towns and the locals stare, some aren't friendly. We also drove past a stall that sells meat and saw some very horrible things like a half skinned sheep hanging by its legs. When you get to the beach you are put into two groups, one gets the catamaran to the island and a speed boat back and the other group the other way round. We were put on the catamaran there, this took about 2 hours. We finally got there and had lunch which was not that nice and then you can sun bathe for a few hours before heading back. When booking this trip we were lead to believe that it was a paradise island but when we got there we realised that the beach back at the hotel was better. We started to wish we hadn't gone but we just decided to go to the bar and drink! Everything seemed to get better, we got on the speedboat back and the drivers race the other speedboats which is quite fun, especially when you've been drinking. They then stop in the middle of the sea and a man jumps out, dives down and picks up star fish for everyone to see. Then you can get out and swim, the sea there is crystal clear and you are able to stand on the bottom even though you are a way out from the shore. Take a snorkle kit on this trip as there are lots of eels and things to see on the bottom. The drivers open the bar again which is an ice box with rum and coke in and everyone relaxes in the sea and drinks. There were about 10 boats there and it seemed like a party in the sea, everyone was singing and having a laugh, this was the best part of the trip. We went quad biking too, this was fun, take sunglasses as they don't tell you to then when you get there they say you can't ride without them and they just so happen to charge alot of money for them there. The staff seem to be quite safe, one rides at the front and the other at the back. They get annoyed if you try and overtake. On the minibus on the way back we stopped at a cross roads and there was a car behind us, the driver handed a gun to one of the men in the minibus and he got off and into the car behind. This was quite scary knowing that the man who had driven you there and back was carrying a gun!! On the way to trips we saw alot of locals with guns. Just carrying them like it was normal. We went to the club in a cave, i've forgotten what it was called but this was ok. It took forever to get there, then it was so hot in there and trying to get a drink was impossible as the locals go here too to party at weekends and the bar staff choose to serve them before tourists. The staff understand no english so learn the spanish word for the drink you like. Its a good idea for a club and the music is good but too hot and crowded.Evening entertainment: Every night there's a show at the stage. Local dancers come in and do shows. It's quite good but gets a bit same old. We would normally play on the pool table as this was near the stage and listen to the shows. Then once the shows had finished there was a disco, very empty as most people go to bed but it was a good place to go and dance and drink if you didn't want to go to bed. Staff: The entertainment staff are very friendly, they speak good english and you always saw them running around keeping the children entertained. The bar staff are a bit moody, they just serve drinks and sometimes you feel as if they are talking about you in their language which is a bit off putting. There was one person who stood out the most, FELIX! He worked on the check in desk, he has the biggest smile and funniest laugh, the first time we met him we wasn't sure what to make of him as we were trying to ask how to use a remote and he just kept laughing at us. We thought he might have been being rude but we went to see him every night after that and he was the nicest person there, he just randomly laughs and always talks to you if he sees you around.Few things:I took my hair straighteners and they didn't work in the room, they required too much power, another couple we met out there had straighteners too but hers worked as they required less power so don't take ghd's, even our plug in mosquito repellents didn't work.By the buffet they have pictures up on the wall, here you can book a photo session with a photographer, you don't have to pay for it just for the photo's you want to buy, this is definatley worth it. The photographs were excellent, we brought ours on a cd as they were cheaper and got them developed back home.On certain days they bring round animals to have your photo taken with, a monkey, parrots and a lizard. You can buy these photo's at the hut too. Take a blockbuster card or points card with you to leave in the key holder in the room, this will leave the air conditioning on for you all day.Try and contact the hotel before you go and request block 5. The rooms are much bigger.Overall:The holiday was excellent for its money. Its not a luxury hotel but the grounds and beach are beautiful. We had a fantastic time and would love to go back.

<Content>Fantastic Time PowBill - Ontario, CanadaDate of Stay: Feb 3rd to 10th, 2008We arrived at Punta Cana airport on Sunday Feb 3rd and were quickly taken to the LTI Beach Resort. The trip was made in a comfortable coach with stops along the way at other hotels. When we arrived at LTI we went to the registration desk to register and were given an upgraded room, Ocean View. The whole check-in experience took about 5 minutes and we were on our way to our room. When we arrived at our room, our luggage was already there. The room was on the ground floor with a view of the ocean. It had 2 twin beds pushed together instead of a king sized. The outside light on the terrace was burned out so we reported it to the registration desk and it was replaced right away. We were quite comfortable in the room and enjoyed sitting on the terrace in the mornings and evenings. The resort is smaller than some that we've stayed in before with fewer bars and restaurants and only 1 swimming pool. We found this to be a good thing as we were able to meet and get to know people better than in a larger resort. In a smaller place, you tend to see the same people every day. We made some good friends and had a wonderful time around and in the pool. The afternoon activies put on by the Activation Team were always entertaining and audiance participation was always a part of it. The drinks were good and the beer was cold. The buffet restaurant had a terrifice selection of food, even the most picky eater should have no problem finding things they like. We didn't try any of the A-la-carte restaurants. The 2nd girl had enthusiam, but missed the whole point of the show which was for the kids to have fun. After the dancing, there would be a contest i.e musical chairs and each night, they would award the prize to like the 8yr old. The contests were WAY TOO competitive. My poor daughter was having fun but got so discouraged as the nights went on that she did not want to participate any more. They would call the people LOSERS and did not have any regard for hurting these young childrens feelings. Plus, one time someone left her purse behind, we told a team member and her reaction was that they can find it themselves. CAN YOU BELIEVE THAT! We took it upon ourselves to find the mom who was grateful to have her purse back. Anyway, overall the Animation team was lacking in customer service and making guests feel GOOD. Seems like they do not want to go out of their way, when i would ask one member about something they ALWAYS would say to go talk to someone else. (4) Front desk. Check in was lame, we arrived in the dark and the front desk guy drew all over the resort map and just left us to find our room by ourselves. Plus, we were suppose to be in a room on the 3rd floor (of a 3 storey building) and when we said that we have 2 kids and a stroller, they VERY reluctantly gave us a room on the main floor. But that room was facing the stage and was very noisy during the night show, and when we asked the next day if they can move us so that our room would not be facing the stage, they said NO because they had accomodated our first request already. We thought that was not a valid reason but they were just too lazy to find us another room. -ROOMS:(1) Very bare - no clock radio ie. alarm. No wash cloths. Bath tub did not drain nor did it plug completely. Water was puddling on the floor (we assumed it came up from the drain in the ground) and I do not think they ever fixed this. (2) Our Mom and Grandmas room smelled of mold. And their TV didnot work. And water was coming down from a sagging ceiling. They told front desk but none of this was fixed right. The one time someone came it to look at the water leaking, they left all their tools and black tar stuff on the floor. Needless to say their Maintenance people were not efficient or effective.- FOOD:(1) Great chicken, bad seafood the entire two weeks. Also, I had some food that was not cooked through, ie shrimp at the Oriental stir fry station and pork kabobs at the grill which I luckily saw before I ate. The workers cooking meat on the grills would use the SAME TONGS to put the raw stuff on the grill as well as on your plate. My husband watched and gestured for him to use the other tongs for the cooked stuff but was ignored so he walked away and ate something else. (2) A la carte restaurants. They had two: seafood and italian. At the seafood one, if you wanted seafood you had to pay extra. Only chicken or beef or pork was included in the all inclusive. At the italian restaurant, the menu was pizzas. Rather lame we thought.(3) For some reason, they did not like giving out milk as a beverage. I would ask for a couple of glasses at lunch and was almost always denied. You would think I was asking for a bottle of Crown Royal or something. Very annoying. And most times they did not have milk with breakfast. And it was never available with dinner. Is milk really more valuable than any alcohol....- BEACH:The sand near and under the lounge chairs was not raked. Full of cigarette butts, drinking straws, and even pieces of glass from beer bottles. A hazard and gross for our kids to play in. - OTHER THOUGHTS:(1) The time share people were always standing outside the entrance to the buffet, so annoying. (2) Room safe was $2USD per day to rent. Internet was $2USD for 15min though the internet cafe was not always open.(3) We thought the night show (at 9:45pm) was too late, we could not go because too late for our kids. Even the mini-disco at 8:30pm, they should try to have it earlier since most kids have an early dinner.(4) One day, we came back to our room to find a notice that they would like to fumigate our room. We called to tell them NO, but how disgusting to think that they would spray pesticides in our room while all our belongings and my babies food was laid out. You would think that they can do this once people are checked out.(5) All the other reviews about the lumpy pillows are right, but you are so tired by night time that it was not a big deal. Overall, LTI is a lovely resort with the most gorgeous beach. I would recommend but would not go back there myself.

<Content>A Mixed Bag This LTI has some good and bad points. The bad points being mainly associated with the room. The resort rooms need a major overhaul. <Author>Mom of one son
<Content>Half 4 star, half 2 star The short version.... the rooms were 2 -3 star at best and the rest of the resort was 4 star and made for a great trip. If you want details why we feel this way.....read on.We traveled on Jan. 4 from Calgary Canada and arrived in a very heavy rain storm. We waited a bit in the lobby to go to the rooms because our luggage was going to get soaked and having arrived at 8 pm this put us at the room after 9. Our conquest agent had not put in our requests to be on anything but a lower floor and had apparently put us in 2 different buildings on the ground floor. The hotel at least put us in the same building as we were travelling as a couple with a 7 year old and my parents in their late 70's but still on the ground floor. They didn't have a bed ready for our son and we only had two twins, so we had to wait for a bed to be put in. We also had no functioning lights beside the beds which is the only real light in the room. They worked on this immediately but it took at least an hour and we were left with black electrician tape holding the bulb in the socket for our entire stay. Both rooms had leaks on our heads from the ceiling above the toilet, and our balcony lock didn't work at all. These problems were fixed more or less. We also had black mold on the ceiling in the bathroom and the wall was falling and chipping into the sink in the bathroom. All the railings outside were badly in need of paint and rusted and wood rot. My parents room had 2 leaks, no lock on the main door besides the flimsy door knob and their toilet flooded once during the week and my mom almost wiped out going to the washroom in the dark. Neither of our tv's received more than 3 channels and these were very fuzzy. They fixed the reception for a day or two then it was gone again. The hotel next door had 30 channels. Overall it seems that the majority of the rooms are literally falling apart but there are a few good ones. The people who get these have a much better view of the hotel. We booked this trip in September so we shouldn't have had the bottom of the barrel. We met many people at the pool who had similiar or worse experiences with the rooms and any that they changed to were as bad or worse. We also both found that the maids opened the balcony doors when cleaning the rooms and left them unlocked. We left notes to please lock them but it seemed that the staff changed daily and it ended up happening almost everyday. We didn't have anything go missing but we didn't exactly have high end stuff in the room.That said, once you got out of your room if you got one of the 2 star versions.........the pool, beach, ocean, staff and meals were all at least 4 star from my previous experiences in the D.R or Cuba. The al a carte's are a little below par for menu selection but at least we never once in 2 weeks had to wait for a table or line up for food or reservations we also always found pool chairs until a large group of europeans turned up and reserved everything and didn't use it all day. There were still pool chairs, just no shade areas left. The animacion staff was a blast and the shows were pretty good were never saw the same one in 14 nights and a couple were really professionally done. Our bar and restaurant service was always very good and yes a lot don't speak English in these areas but a smile is a smile! We made some good friends with the staff but did have problems with reception staff with trying to change rooms after the first night. We were told to come back in two days that lots of rooms would be opening up but when I showed up at 10 am. as requested, they were all gone, it was come back tomorrow at 1, then the next day until finally we just got what we could fixed in our existing rooms as best as possible and finally unpacked.If you go not expecting much from the rooms you won't be disappointed but ours were on par with a 2 star US hotel. You can tell that once upon a time they were very nice but the maintainance has been non-existent and stays that way unless you complain. We did hear that the hotel has been bought out by the time share and they are to renovate next summer. If that is true and it is a full renovation, then we would love to go back when it is done. Otherwise, no way without staying at the Cayene Beach club instead.In closing, we will always look at our outdoor shots to have good memorys of this trip and the people like Pablo, Soniylla, Pedro, Aureillio and Beinvenito. Sylvie at the front desk was also very helpful with at least getting the big stuff fixed in our rooms.If you are going, just remember to put the room behind you if you get ones like we did!

<Content>well worth the money some people expect way too much. Myself and my boyfriend stayed here from 24th September til the 8th October. We had prepared ourselves for the worst but were suprised when we got there as to how lovely the resort really was. Check-in went smoothly and quickly, the staff were very friendly, and as other guests have done we emailed the hotel and asked for building 5 and thats what we got. Our room was massive, a huge kingsize bed, tv with more than enough english channels so if we wanted to watch it we could. We also had a pull out sofa bed which we didnt need but used as a sitting area. The maid came in daily and cleaned as well as refilling our fridge with 2 cokes 2 sprites and 2 large bottles of water. The hotel gardens were kept immaculate and the beach was only a 30 second walk from our room. The beach has extremely white sand and clear warm waters. My boyfriend went out and fed the fish bread as did many other people, he was surrounded by hundreds of them - you only have to gout into waist high water. The hotels pool wasnt as clean as we would of liked as we often found bugs in the pool but only after there had been a storm over night and by afternoon someone would of cleaned it out anyway. The main buffet resturant had more than enough choice, with a pasta station, chinese station etc where you pick what you want and the chef cooks it in front of you. Also there is the same sort of thing at breakfast with omlettes. We didnt try the seafood a la carte but we did try the italian which was really nice. We went there about 8 times in the 2 weeks we were there, the lasagne is gorgeous. They also do a seafood night at the beach on fridays where they make it look all romantic it looks lovely but we dont like fish so didnt bother. You have to try a bananamama cocktail, and also their pina coladas are good. Also go to the lobby and meet felix behind the information desk - he will initially just laugh at you but it is so funny to watch, we stood talking to him for hours, although some americans got offended he doesnt mean any harm. Michael Jackson show is really good the best of the evening entertainment. Recommend Saona island and quad biking, also the tropicana nightclub for those 18-30 if you want a strange but good nite out in a club in an underground cave (the more of you that go on one booking the less they will charge pp). Me neither my boyfriend got ill, only with a hangover, so anyone who did was probably a hypochondriac, or just being picky. The staff make you feel welcome and do not expect tips, but it is nice to give them as they genuinely appreciate even one dollar. We paid 拢700 pp for our holiday and it was worth every penny. I really dont understand so many negative reviews from the americans.

<Author>Samiantha
<Content>The perfect beach for the perfect holiday... We booked this hotel on teletext holidays and got a pretty good deal compared to Airtours.Myself, boyfriend (both aged 22) and my parents stayed at the hotel for 2 weeks from the 17th September. All of us had a brillant time and would, without a doubt go back. We had paid the extra to get the sea view rooms and were not disappointed. We were on the ground floor (rooms 5014 and 5019) rooms. Looking into the standard rooms we had a far bigger room, with the room including a mini sitting room (which we didn't really need). From the room, I would say we were about 10m from the sea - perfect when waking up in the morning and opening your curtains - you felt that you were on a maladives island! The rooms were a little basic, however suited the purpose of sleeping! Reading other reviews, and the complaints about the toilets - we didn't have a problem!The food was brillant and throughout the 2 weeks we didn't get bored or struggle finding things to eat. We have stayed in a lot of AI before and I have to say the buffet was the best. The stir fry station was yummy with you being able to choice how much and what you wanted. The pasta station was also the same. Some days the roast station the meat was a bit tough - but the turkey was brill. We went to both al carte resturants, however felt the sea food resturant was a waste of time. The italian was superb, with the best pizza's and lasagne I've tasted in a long time - so good that we went here 3 times!We didn't spend much time around the pool however it was always busy with little children with the childrens pool well sheltered with palm trees. Most of our time was spent on the beach. Our spot of beach was by far the best bit of beach! The sea was that lovely blue colour, some days it was slightly cloudy so snorkeling was hard but most of the time we saw lovely coloured fish. You don't need to take your snorkels as you can get them from the watersports station for an hr each day for free as well as flippers. Also we took bread rolls out and you got soooo many fish eating from you :-)We did two trips - the trip to the Island and the caribbean festival. The Island trip was good, the sea was a lovely blue however we were disappointed with the sea as there was huge bits of coral near the edge so it made it difficult to get in and out. On the way back we did the starfish bit. It was interesting to see them, however we only found a couple so were led slightly astray on seeing the hundreds which we were promised. This trip took all day where we were picked up at 7am and didn't get back till gone 6pm with a good 1hr30min drive to the port. The caribbean festival was brillant. First stop was a coral reef followed by a swim with sharks and stingrays. The staff on the boat did a fantastic job and we would do it again. In terms of shopping you won't find a lot apart from the usual tourist bits. We found the lamire (blue stone) very over priced so you have to haggle a far bit. Your best bet would be to get the brugal rum. All in all we had a brill holiday, and without a doubt would go back in a flash - we landed in Gatwick and wanted the plane to turn around!

<Author>Garry_and_Lorna
<Content>Great Family Holiday Firstly, I have got to say, some of these reviews I have read on here from some guys from the USA are a little harsh to say the least. There where 5 people in our party 2 couples aged 21-24  a 5 year old. On arrival the hotel is very clean and gleaming and the bell boys greet you with a smile and a chilled drink, which comes in handly after a long flight from Manchester (UK). Upon getting to our room, first thoughts were that it was a little basic but there was everything there that you need. There was a hair-dryer in the bathroom which my Girlfriend informs me was pretty decent, a TV, with a few English speaking channels, but you dont go on holiday to watch TV do you? There was also a mini bar, which was stocked up with Coke, Sprite and Water daily from the maid, which come in handy after a day lounging round the pool. The beds were a little hard, and the pillows a little lumpy, however over 14 nights never caused too many problems. The maid kept the room nice and clean, and was always very pleasent when we met her. We chose to tip her one dollar a day, we in no way felt obliged to do this, but we just wanted to show our gratitude for the job she was doing. In return she left nice little flowers and treats around the room. Next....The Restaurants. We ate in 4 of the restaurants. Firstly, 'El Mirador' aka the buffet retaurant......Breakfast was ok, a good variety of food on offer, not all was to our taste but there was enough there to suit everyone. The bread for the toast seemed a little stale, however this may be due to the heat  lack of A/C. Chef's are on hand cooking fresh Pancakes, and omelettes to your liking. There is are also fresh milkshakes made which are delicious. We didnt actually eat there for lunch, as we chose to stay around the pool, but the buffet selection for Dinner again varied and there was enough to suit everyone. There are fresh meats on a carvery, and fish cooked to order. The meat does tend to be a little rare though. There are Chef's on hand cooking pasta on request and the Stir fry is to die for. Our faverate restaurant was the Italian, which offers deicious pizza's lasgne, etc and were a nice change to the buffet. Under no circumstances were the staff in any restaurant rude or obnoxious towards us, and there is no way they made you feel like there is an obligation to tip. They top up your drinks all night always with a smile. None of our party were ill apart from the odd sniffle and dodgy belly which didnt last more than a day and no way stopped us from doing anything.The pool and beach were very very good. There is a nice relaxed atmosphere at both and the days just roll into one when you are relaxing. The pool is lovely and warm and was never really overly crowded. There were always sun beds and there is a great grill serving, chicken, burgers etc all day which are lovely. The entertainment team are the stars of the place and work there socks off, always pleasent and always energentic. Every day they change the stage layouts from top to bottom which isn't a 5 min job, aswell as supervising varuous activities throughout the day. The night-time shows are always varied and provided some great moments for us over the 14 nights in particular the Comedy show and the Magic Show. If i was to score the team on there own I would give them 6/5! They played a major part in our enjoyment of the holiday.All in all, i am gald i did not pay too much attention to some of the reviews on this site, as we all had the time of our lives at the LTI.

<Author>oswegomrsbaker
<Content>Great Value for families Last Christmas, my family decided to have a mini family reunion in The Dominican Republic. We decided to go to Punta Cana because the beaches are better. We chose LTI because of the price and amenities for the price. First, the positive...It has a wonderful beach, especially for younger children. It is on a part of the beach where the waves are not as rough. If you are like my husband, who likes big waves, it is only a five minute walk down the beach to bigger waves. It is also a little further down the beach from the rest of the resorts, so it is more private and less crowded. The pool was nice and never crowded. there was a perfect size wading pool for toddlers.THere are many bars that had great choices of drinks and cocktails. Everyday there were numerous activities around that had food different from the buffet. This food tneded to be much better that what was at the buffet.The two reservation required, but still inclusive, restaurants had very good food. OUr family really enjoyed the Italian restaurant. The rooms were clean and the staff was very friendly and attentive. When checking in ask for the newer building on the beach. A lot of the rooms overlook the beach with wonderful views. They are closest to the beach and are newly renovated. There are a lot of activities that can be arranged from the resort. We did parasailing, horseback riding, ATV tours, catamaran, snorkeling, and a banan boat. There was much more we could have done but decided to be beach bums the rest of the time.If you go for NEw Year's, all the resort put on a fireworks display. It was really beautiful on the beach!The few negative..The buffet wasn't great if you are a picky eater. Breakfast is good, but the other meals, not so much, A lot of my family members had the typical stomach problems. If you want to play tennis while there, the pro is a little unreliable. They lock the courts after hours, and if you want to play the next day, you have to find the pro to unlock the courts. HE was a very nice and friendly guy, but just hard to find. No one on the resort seems to know where to find him.The resort is one of the furthest from the airport, so it is better to get your own taxi then one of the shuttles that stops at other resorts. It is a great way to get a peek at other resorts, but can get frustrating when you just want to get to you place.IF you go over Christmas, be prepared that on Christmas Eve, Christmas Day, and New Years they close all the restaurants and have a big buffet. But you can't go to the buffet whenver you want, you have to get a seating time. We arrived on Christmas Eve and received a seating of 8:30, which wasn't great for my 13 month old. All in all, it was a good resort for the money. It wasn't as large and luxurious as some of the other resorts. IT is still a great vacation, and one of the best beach locations in Punta Cana

<Author>alpinegato
<Content>Nice Vacation, Great Value, Had a Good Time My husband, 14 yr old daughter and I stayed at the LTI the last week in June. We got a really good last minute deal and the price was right. The weather was great the entire week we were there. It rained only at night so it didn't bother us. One night there was a terrific thunder and lightning storm which we heard was very unusual. Arrival: We were able to check in quickly and smoothly. Our luggage arrived in our room about 10 minutes after we did. I too had read the previous travelers' reviews and was a little bit worried about certain experiences they had. I followed someone's advice and sent a fax a few weeks before our arrival requesting either Building #4 or #5. We got building # 5, third floor with an ocean view! Another surprise was the plate of fresh fruit and place setting for two along with a small complimentary bottle of Rum waiting in our room when we got there! (Maybe they thought I was a travel agent?) The room was nice and they had also set up an additional bed for us for my daughter! So our welcome was first rate and we were impressed. The AC was also on when we got there. Restaurants: Once you got used to the various dishes being served at the buffet, we could find something we liked. The Oriental Stir Fry station at dinner was very good and the Omelet station for breakfast was also very good. There were plenty of pastries and fruit to pick from. Their cold cuts are different and so are their hot dogs. At lunch we ate at the poolside restaurant/grill. The chicken is great! It is like a rotisserie chicken seasoned really well. They serve hamburgers and French fries there all day long too. There is no problem booking a reservation at the two specialty restaurants each morning at breakfast. We liked both the Italian one where they had a nice lasagna and good pizza and the Seafood restaurant which was air-conditioned and offered a really good seafood soup or French onion soup as an appetizer! Activities: We did a little bit of snorkeling on the beach and saw some neat fish. The animation team is very energetic and do their best at trying to get people involved in activities and games. They work long and hard hours. We played BINGO at the pool and won a bottle of rum! The nightly entertainment is ok. A few of the shows were really good including the 鈥淢ichael Jackson鈥?show and the magic show. If you tip the waiters at the Theater they will come back and take care of you all night. After the show they serve some pretty good sandwich snacks at the Calypso Bar right next door.My daughter and I took the Tropical Storm catamaran trip off the beach which I HIGHLY recommend to anyone. It was awesome. You can book it at the Dive Shop on the beach it costs about $84 if you pay cash, more if by credit card. It was well worth it. They feed you on the boat and provide you with drinks after you are done snorkeling. The fish we saw were amazing, all colors and we were able to feed them right out of our hands!Other: The pillows are flat, lumpy etc. and we asked our maid the 2nd day for 3 extra pillows which helped.The grounds are beautiful, vegetation is mature, the pools are nice and the beach is great too. Very soft sand, no shells. Bring bug spray! I was bitten every night at the theater by something which left painful itchy welts which lasted a few days.
